/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/ScriptRuntime.html:2982: The order of evaluation of an assignment expression involves
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/ScriptRuntime.html:2983: evaluating the lhs to a reference, evaluating the rhs, and then
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/ScriptRuntime.html-2984- modifying the reference with the rhs value. This method is used
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/ScriptRuntime.html-2985- to 'bind' the given name to an object containing that property
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/ScriptRuntime.html:2986: so that the side effects of evaluating the rhs do not affect
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/ScriptRuntime.html-2987- which property is modified.

/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/commonjs/module/provider/ModuleSourceProviderBase.html-370-<div class="block">Override to determine whether according to the validator, the cached
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/commonjs/module/provider/ModuleSourceProviderBase.html:371: module script needs revalidation. A validator can carry expiry
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/commonjs/module/provider/ModuleSourceProviderBase.html-372- information. If the cached representation is not expired, it doesn'
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/commonjs/module/provider/ModuleSourceProviderBase.html:373: t need revalidation, otherwise it does. When no cache revalidation is
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/commonjs/module/provider/ModuleSourceProviderBase.html-374- required, the external resource will not be contacted at all, so some
##############################################
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/commonjs/module/provider/ModuleSourceProviderBase.html-376- The default implementation always returns true so it will always require
/src/deps/rhino/docs/org/mozilla/javascript/commonjs/module/provider/ModuleSourceProviderBase.html:377: revalidation.</div>
